taṁpi hu parivāhaṁtō vēēṇaṁ jāi dūradēsammi । tattha ya kahiṁci paḍiyaṁ kaṇṇāō kuṁḍalaṁ sahasā ॥6॥5801 ॥

sōūṇa taō dhammaṁ, vaṁdittā bhaṇai muṇivaraṁ ēsō । 'bhayavaṁ ! gihammi gaṁtu, sutthaṁ kāūṇa savvaṁ pi ॥ 42 ॥ 5837॥

ētō purōhiṇaṁ vijāsāmatthaō narēṁdassa । sīsammi kayā viyaṇā duvvisahā pāyayanarāṇaṁ ॥ 18 ॥ 5869 ॥
tō raṇṇā saddittā purōhiō jaṁpiō jahā 'bhadda ! । sīsammi majjha viyaṇā uppannā dāruṇā aja' ||19|| 5870 ।।

jaha 'bhadda ! tumaṁ vaccasu dīvē kiṁjaṁpināmadhēyammi । kiṁjaṁpisauṇagāṇaṁ āṇayaṇatthaṁ surūvāṇaṁ' ||25|| 5876 ॥

bhaṇiyā paccaiyanarā 'purōhiō jai kahiṁci iha ēi । baṁdhittā pacchannaṁ, tō āṇējjāha maha pāsē ॥ 28 ॥ 5879 ।।

jaṁpai guru vi 'bhaddē ! mā hu pamāyaṁ karējjasu khaṇaṁ pi' । 'icchaṁ' ti bhāṇiūṇaṁ jāi imā tattha ṭhāṇammi ॥ 61 ॥ 6161॥
jattha jaṇayāiyāṇaṁ sayaṇasamaggāṇa vaṭṭai vivāō । vinnavai 'mā vivāyaṁ karēha ēyammi kajjammi || 62||6162॥
jamhā hu savvaviraī ajja gahissāmi gurusamīvammi । jēṇaṁ tumha vivāō phiṭṭai ēyammi visayammi' || 63 ॥ 6163 ॥
iya jaṁpiyammi sayaṇō bhaṇai 'ahō ! kannayāvivēō tti । jēppa vivāyaṁ dahuṁ, muṁcai savvaṁ pi visayasuhaṁ ॥ 64 ॥ 6164 ॥
tā ēyaṁ ciya juttaṁ imammi ēvaṁvihammi patthāvē । ahahē ! imō nivvaliō suhaiṇa visamō vi hu vivāō' ॥65॥6165 ॥
mannittā tavyayaṇaṁ vivāhasāmaggiyaṁ paricaiuṁ । āḍhavai tīē dikkhāsāmaggiṁ mahavibhūīē ॥ 66 ॥ 6166 ॥
taṁ daddhuṁ vaddhāvayapurisā vi viṇiggayā vimaṇamaṇasā । gaṁtūṇa imaṁ savvaṁ niyaniyalōyāṇa akkhati ॥67॥6167॥
sōūṇaṁ takkahiyaṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ tē kumāracaurō vi । taduvari daḍhāṇurāyā niyaniyagēhāī pai valiyā ॥ 68 ॥ 6168॥
daṭuṇa aṁtarālammi tāvasē lēti tāṇa dikkhāō । mittāṇaṁ lajaṁtā na gayā niyaēsu gēhēsu ॥ 69 ॥ 6169 ॥

kaṇikāiyaṁ payaṁtī, kuṇaṁti taha sālaṇāiyaṁ kiṁci । ēvaṁ siddhāē rasavaīē aha bhōyaṇanimittaṁ ॥ 46 ॥ 6255 ॥

ēvaṁ ca bhōyaṇavāulāṇaṁ pamattayāṇaṁ satthillaya narāṇaṁ cārapurisēhiṁtō viyāṇiūṇa bhillasaṁghāyā 'haṇa haṇa haṇa' tti
gaddabhavayaṇasammissapaḍahayasiṁgayārāvabhayakarā nivaḍiyā tammi satthē । taō asēsaniyapurisaparivuḍō sannaddhabaddhakavaō—
'rē rē durāyārabhillā ! purisā havējjāha' tti bhaṇamāṇō laggō jujjhiuṁ sulasō । jāva khaṇamēkkaṁ jujjhai tāva thōvattaṇaō "
āḍattiyāṇaṁ, aipabhūyattaṇaō ya bhillāṇaṁ bhēlliō saṁghāō, pāḍiyā āḍattiyanarā hayasēsā ya naṭṭhā। sulasō vi
purisakāramamuṁcaṁtō gahiō pharaēhiṁ ōhaḍiūṇa nīō sabhavaṇē । taō 'pabhūyaṇiyasuhaḍaviṇāsagō' tti ruṭṭhēhiṁ vikkīō
parakūlagāmimahaṇasatthavāhasamīvē । tēṇa vi nīō parakūlē, davvalōbhēṇa ya vikkiō ṇēṇa । 'uvaciyagattō' tti gahiō
māṇusaruhiratthiṇā tavvatthavvagēṇa । tattha ya māṇusaruhirēṇa kijjaē kimirāgō, avi ya
pōsittu māṇusāī savvaṁga paṁcchiūṇa gālēṁtiṁ । taddēhāō ruhiraṁ kuṁḍīō bharaṁti tē rōddā ॥48॥6257||

sulasō vi bhaṇai 'naṇu maṁciyāē hēṭummi tāiṁ baddhāī । tā uttārēhi mamaṁ, jēṇa suhaṁ tāī chōḍēmi ' ॥ 95 ॥ 6304॥

jaṁ ca ghasaṁtō paḍiō taṁ dukkhaviō na tārisaṁ kiṁpi । bhaṇai ya mahasaddēṇaṁ 'namō jiṇāṇaṁ' ti bhāvēṇa ॥100॥6309 ॥
" hā jīva pāvakammaya ! jai taiya cciya taē vayaṁ gahiyē । hutaṁ āsi taō taṁ ṇa ya pāvēṁtō imaṁ vasaṇaṁ ॥ 101 ॥6310॥
hā jīva ! jai gurūṇaṁ hiyāṇa sikkhā taē kayā hōtā। tō na hu iya dukkhāṇaṁ bhāyaṇamaṇahaṁ tumaṁ hutō' ॥102॥6311॥
hā jīva ! jai ṇivittī pariggahāō taē kayā hōtā । tā na hu ēttha paḍatō narayāgārammi kūvammi ॥ 103 ॥ 6312 ॥
tā iṇhi pi na naṭuṁ gahiūṇaṁ savvaviraisāmannaṁ । gēṇhasu aṇasaṇamaṇahaṁ jēṇa'ja vi tarasi saṁsāraṁ" ॥104॥6313॥ 10
iya vōttūṇaṁ jā lēi aṇasaṇaṁ savvaviraisaṁjuttaṁ । tā hēṭṭhillayapurisēṇa vāriō 'mā imaṁ kuṇasu' ॥ 105 ॥ 6314 ॥

1. khaḍahāē jē0 kā 0 ॥ 2. divvajō kā0 | dēvajō pā0 ॥। 3. hōtō pā0 ॥। 4. jēṇēvaṁ vā jē0 kā0 ||

'jaya jaya naṁdā, jaya jaya bhaddā, jaya naṁda naṁda suciraṁ ti । amhāṇa tumaṁ sāmī tujjha 'mhē kiṁkarā dēva ! ॥ 197 ॥ 6406 ॥
tā dāyavya amhaṁ āēsō ṇicamēva tumbhēhiṁ' । iya nisuṇatō ciṁtai " kahamētthamahaṁ samuppannō ॥ 198 ॥ 6407॥
savyuttama kaṁtidharō, savyuttamarūvasaṁpayā kaliō । savyuttamaparivārō, savyuttamariddhivitthārō ? ॥ 199 ॥ 6408 ॥
tā kiṁ dinna dāṇaṁ ? kiṁvā vi tavaṁ visiṭuyaṁ taviyaṁ ? । kiṁ vā dhariyaṁ sīlaṁ ? vibhāviyā bhāvaṇā kiṁ vā ? '॥200॥6409॥
ēvaṁ ciṁtaṁtēṇaṁ sahasā viṣphāriyaṁ avahināṇaṁ । diṭuṁ kūvayamajjhē kaḍēvaraṁ rasaparikkhaiyaṁ ॥ 201 ||6410 ॥

pālēttu saṁjama sō saṁpattē maraṇadēsakālammi । aṇasaṇavihiṇā mariuṁ saṁpattō dēvalōgammi” ॥30॥6593 ॥

tā paribhōgē ēvaṁ aparimiē dūsaṇaṁ muṇēūṇa । kuṇaha sayā parimāṇaṁ ubabhōgē taha ya paribhōgē || 1 ||6648 ॥
taiyaṁ guṇavvayaṁ puṇa aṇatthaḍaṁḍassa hōi jā viraī । taṁ bhiṛaṁtaṁ kamasō caubhēyaṁ hōi vinnēyaṁ ||2||6649॥
tattha ya jaṁ avajhāṇaṁ paḍhamō bhēō imō muṇēyabbō । jaṁ tu pamāyācariyaṁ taṁ bīyaṁ muṇaha bhēyavasā || 3 || 6650॥
hiṁsappayāṇanāmaṁ taijjayaṁ, pāvakammauvaēsō । hōi cautthō ēyaṁ aṇatthadaṁḍavvayasarūvaṁ ॥4॥ 6651 ॥
।
advēṇa taṁ na vajjhai, vajjhai jamaṇaṭuō u kira pāvaṁ । kālāīyā aṭṭhē niyāmagā, jō aṇaṭṭāē ॥ 5 ॥ 6652 ॥

mōhariyaṇāma taiō, cautthaō saṁjuyāhigaraṇaṁ tu । ubabhōga parībhōgē airēgō paṁcama'iyārō ॥ 7 ॥ 6654॥
ētthaṁ pi udāharaṇaṁ kahēmi tumhāṇa kiṁci lēsēṇaṁ । “ dhāyaisaṁḍē dīvē bhārahakhēttammi supasiddhaṁ ॥ 1 ॥6655 ॥
atthi puraṁ pōrāṇaṁ kaṇagapuraṁ nāma dasadisipayāsaṁ । taṁ paripālai rāyā payaḍō riumaddaṇō nāma ॥ 2 ॥ 6656 ॥
tassa ya bhajjā aṁtēurassa majjhammi jāu supasiddhā । kēusirī nāmēṇaṁ acaṁtaṁ suṁdarāvayavā ॥3॥6657 ॥
tattha ya samiddhadattō nivasai kōḍubiō suvikkhāō । pālai niyayakuḍuṁba niyakulakamavittikaraṇēṇaṁ ॥ 4 ॥ 6658 ॥

" jai majjha hōi rajjaṁ tō haṁ rāyā bhavāmi vikkhāō । sāhēmi taō savvaṁ chakkhaṁḍaṁ bharahavāsamiṇaṁ ||6 ॥ 6660 ॥

tattha ya vēyaḍḍhanagē jē kēvi hu atthi khēyarā savvē । tē maha āṇākārī hōhiṁti na ēttha saṁdēhō ||7|| 6661॥
tō haṁ tē āṇāē vaṭṭaṁtē ēvamālavissāmi । jaha dēha bhadda ! majjha vijāō aṇaṇṇasarisāō || 8 || 6662॥

kāūṇaṁ uḍissaṁ, bijāō sumariūṇa gacchissaṁ" । iya āvēsavasēṇaṁ uṭṭhittā dēi sō phālaṁ ॥ 11 ॥ 6665 ॥
āyāsayaphālēṇaṁ paḍiō dharaṇīyalammi sahasa tti । dukkhāviō ya ahiyaṁ savvēsu vi aṁguvaṁgēsu || 12 || 6 6 6 6 ॥
vēyaṇavihurō tāhē akkaṁdai bhūtalammi luḍhamāṇō । tō māṇusēhiṁ uppāḍiūṇa sijāē saṁviō ॥13॥6667॥
mahayā kaṭṭēṇa taō kaha kahavi hu vēyaṇā uvassaṁtā । jāō satthasarīrō pālēi puṇō vi niyagēhaṁ ॥ 14 ॥ 6668 ॥
ēttō ya tassa khaggaṁ suṁdararūvaṁ maṇōharaṁ atthi । bahudavvēṇaṁ kīyaṁ supasiddhaṁ tammi visayammi || 15 ||6 6 69 ॥
taṁ puṇa khaggaṁ bāhiṁ nirūvaṇatthaṁ tu kaḍriḍhayaṁ āsi । taṁ pi hu pamāyadōsā vīsariyaṁ bāhirē cēva ॥ 16 ॥ 6670 ॥
rayaṇīē paharadugē gayammi majjhaṭṭhiēṇa saṁbhaliyaṁ । taha vi pamāyavasēṇaṁ na uṭṭhiūṇaṁ kayaṁ majjhē ||17|| 6671 ॥
"jaha kira pabhāyakālē prāṇammi imaṁ ahaṁ karissāmi" । iya ciṁtiūṇa suttō niddapamāēṇa akkaṁtō ॥18॥ 6672 ॥
1. sējāē pā0 vinā ॥ 2. ca jē0 ॥

<pb n="600 plus 196"/>

ētthaṁtarammi kamavi rayaṇīē pacchimammi jāmammi । divvavasēṇa paviṭṭhā cōrā gēhammi aha tassa ॥ 19॥6673॥
gahiyaṁ ca tayaṁ khaggaṁ cōrēhiṁ uggayammi tō sūrē । "taṁ jāva nirūvēṁtī tā ṇāyaṁ khaggarayaṇamiṇaṁ ॥ 20॥6674 ॥
" tō gēṇhāmō kiṁcī vaṁdammi jēṇa hōi sahalamiṇaṁ" । iya ciṁtiūṇa gahiō baṁdēṇaṁ nayarasēṭṭisuō ॥21॥ 6675 ॥
baṁdiyapurisēhiṁ samaṁ sēdvisuō tattha pāviō maraṇaṁ । dadūṇa tayaṁ khaggaṁ bhaṇati lōyā taō payaḍaṁ ||22||6676 ॥
" ēyaṁ taṁ varakhaggaṁ samiddhadattassa saṁtiyaṁ jaṁ tu । ḍhukkaṁ ca naravaissā" tēṇa vi hakkāriō ēsō ॥ 23 ॥ 6677॥
'rē pāvakamma ! niddaya ! kayaṁ taē ērisaṁ kimēyaṁ ?' ti । sō āha 'ēyakammāṇa kāraō dēva ! na hu ahayaṁ' ||24|| 6678 ॥
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ 'jai na vi tō kiṁ ēyaṁ tuhatayaṁ khaggaṁ ? ' । sō bhaṇai 'dēva ! mā kuppa suṇasu vinnattiyaṁ majjha ॥ 25॥6679॥
ēyaṁ viyālakālē kallaṁ rayaṇīē bāhi vīsariyaṁ । taṁ cōrēhiṁ nīyaṁ khaggaṁ iya vilasiyaṁ tāṇa ॥ 26 ॥ 6680॥
jai puṇa ahamēyāṇaṁ kammāṇaṁ kāraō taō dēva ! । duṭṭēṇa vi divvēṇaṁ pattijjāvēmi nīsaṁkaṁ' ॥27॥6681 ॥
ēvaṁ piṁ hu paḍibhaṇiē rāyā tō taṁ pamāyadōsēṇaṁ । daṁḍēūṇaṁ mēllai jīvaṁtaṁ gahiyasavvassaṁ ॥ 28 ॥ 6682 ॥
ēttō puṇō vi kālē jaṁtē aha kēttiyammi vi samiddhō । jāō samiddhadattō puvvaṁ va samiddhibhārēṇa ॥ 29॥6683 ॥
annamma diṇē purisēṇa kaha vi ēgēṇa maggiō ēsō । jaha 'jaṁ tumaē gahiyaṁ visaṁ taō dēhi mē kiṁci' ॥ 30 ॥6684 ॥
1. nirūvaṁti pā0 vinā ॥। 2. vi tru0 kā0 ॥। 3. aha nāsti tru0 ॥

tēṇa vi dinnaṁ maggatayassa, tattō visāō thōvayaraṁ । tēṇa vi taṁ gahiūṇaṁ talāṁyamajjhammi pakkhittaṁ ॥ 31 ॥ 6685 ॥
jēṇa nivō marai imō saha lōgēṇaṁ jaō imō purisō । rāyassa vēriēṇaṁ paṭuviō rāyavahaṇatthaṁ ॥ 32 ॥6686 ॥
tattō vi jāba lōgō uggavvisabhāviēṇa nīrēṇa । kēttiyamēttō vi tahiṁ paṁcattaṁ pāviō jhatti ॥ 33 ॥ 6687 ॥
taṁ daṇaṁ raṇṇā jāva ya niuṇaṁ gavēsiyaṁ tāva । kahiyaṁ kēṇa vi raṇṇō samiddhadattassa taṁ cariyaṁ ||34||6688॥
puṇaravi hakkāritā bhaṇiō 'rē pāva ! kiṁ kayaṁ ēyaṁ ?' । sō bhaṇai 'dēva ! jāṇāmi nēva kēṇā'vi kayamēyaṁ ॥ 35 ॥6689 ॥
kiṁtu ahaṁ ēgēṇaṁ purisēṇaṁ maggiō jahā majjha । atthi mahaṁtaṁ kajaṁ, tā maha thōvaṁ visaṁ dēhi || 36 ||6690॥
dinnaṁ ca maē sijjhau paōyaṇaṁ naṇu mahāṇubhāvassa । na ya mē dudusahāvō viyāṇiō dēva ! muddhēṇaṁ' ॥37॥6691॥
'hiṁsappayāṇakāri' tti puṇa vi kuddhēṇa rāiṇā tassa । savvassaṁ avahariyaṁ mukkō sō jīvamēttēṇa ॥ 38 ॥ 6692 ॥
ēvaṁ sō vi hu duhiō jāva'cchai kaivi vāsarē tāva । puvyakayakammavasaō saṁjāyā puṇaravi samiddhī ॥ 39 ॥ 6693 ।।
avarammi vāsarammiṁ parisāē jāva ciṭui niviṭṭhō । tā tēṇaṁ aṁtēṇaṁ bōlai kōḍubiō ēkkō ॥ 40 ॥ 6994॥
karagahiyapavara kalhōḍajubalaō pēcchiūṇa taṁ bhaṇai । 'bhō ! bhō ! damiyā kiṁ nō ēē kalhōḍayā tumaē ? ' ॥41॥6695॥
sō bhaṇai 'nēya ajja vi' samiddhadattō payaṁpaē ēttō । 'jai ēvaṁ, tō bhaddaya ! mā kuṇasu pamāyamētthatthē ॥ 42 ॥ 6696॥
1. lāvama° tru0 ॥ 2. kittiya tru0 ॥। 3. hakkārēttā tru0 jē0 ॥। 4. nēya tru0 kā0 ।। 5. ēgō kā0 ||

damasu imē dō vi tumaṁ jēṇaṁ jōgā halassa jāyaṁti । tā ārā vēhāīhiṁ damasu ainiddaō hōuṁ ॥ 43 ॥ 6697॥
pōsiti na kēvalamēē taha niḍurēṇa cittēṇa । añcatthaṁ damasu imē jēṇa na macaṁti' parijuttā ॥44॥6698 ॥
ēyaṁ niravayaṇaṁ dōha vi kalhōḍayāṇa savaṇēsu । paḍiyaṁ tēṇaṁ ca taō tē dō vi hu dummaṇā jāyā ||45 || 6699 ॥
ciṁtaṁti “imaṁ pāvaṁ ainiḍurabhāsayaṁ viṇāsēmō । jō amhāṇaṁ pīḍaṁ uvaisai suniddaō hōuṁ" ॥46॥6700॥
ēvaṁ ciṁtaṁtā tē nīyā gōsāmiēṇa niyagēhē । gōsāmiō vi cittē taṁ vayaṇaṁ nicchiyaṁ dhariuṁ ॥ 47 ॥6701 ॥
annamma diṇē tēṇaṁ āḍhattā dō vi vāhi ṁ basahā । ainiddayacittēṇaṁ viṁdhai tikkhāhiṁ ārāhiṁ ॥48॥ 6702 ॥
tē viha vāraṁ vāraṁ vidhijētā maṇammi kuppati । vāhicaṁtā ya daḍhaṁ sukumālattā u tē tuṭṭā ॥49॥6703 ॥
tē tuṭṭē nāūṇaṁ āsa mēllēi tāṇa sō sāmī । vasahā vi marēūṇaṁ dōnni vi. aha vaṁtarā jāyā ||50 || 6704 ॥
khōḍēūṇaṁ kammaṁ vivihāē akāmanijarāē u । tattō uvavannēhiṁ dōhiṁ vi vitthāriyaṁ nāṇaṁ ॥ 51 ॥ 6705 ।।
diṭṭhāī dēhāī maraṇassa ya kāraṇaṁ taō nāyaṁ । taṁ jāṇiūṇa ruṭṭhā samiddhadattassa uvarimmi ॥ 52 ॥ 6706॥
āgaṁtūṇa ya dōnni vi dēhē nāṇāvihāō viyaṇāō । uppāyaṁti sukuddhā bhaṇati aha niduraṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 53॥6707 ॥
'rē rē niḍurabhāsaga ! niddaya ! nittiṁsa ! kūrakammāṇa ! । taiyā ēvaṁ bhaṇatō kiṁ jāṇasi ? sahasu tā iṇhi' ॥54॥6708॥
1. upā0 ।। 2. nāuṁ pā0 ।।

ēvaṁ samiddhadattō viyaṇāhiṁ pīḍiō aṇēgāhiṁ । sōūṇa tiyasavayaṇaṁ jōḍiyakarasaṁpuḍō bhaṇai ॥ 55 ॥6709 ॥
'dēva ! pasīyaha majjha avarāhaṁ khamaha jēṇa sappurisā । paṇivaiyavacchala cciya bhavaṁti tumhārisā nūṇaṁ ॥ 56॥6710॥
tā haṁ dhūva - kaḍacchuyahatthō tumhāṇa saṁpayaṁ jāō' । iya sōūṇaṁ dōnni vi kōvaṁ muṁcati tē tiyasā ॥57॥6711 ॥
uvasaṁhari ṁ viyaṇāō tāō vaccēti niyayāṇammi । viyaṇāmukkō saṁtō ciṁtai ēsō vi cittēṇa ॥58॥6712 ।।
" hā jiya ! avajhāṇēṇaṁ paḍiēṇa tumē sudāruṇaṁ dukkhaṁ । aṇuhūyaṁ puṇa pacchā pamāyakaraṇassa dōsēṇa ॥ 59॥65713 ॥
savvassaṁ avahariyaṁ rannā tattō ya hiṁsadāṇēṇa । puṇa savvassa'vahārō tumaē rē pāviō jīva ! ||60||6714 ॥
pāvayauvaēsēṇaṁ iṇhi jāō puṇō vi duhakhāṇī । tā pariharāhi ēē caurō vi aṇatthaḍaṁḍē u” ॥ 61 ॥6715॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa baccai ēsō sirisūripāyamūlammi । giṇhai aṇubbayāīsāvagadhammaṁ supaḍipuṇṇaṁ ॥ 62 ॥6716 ॥
aṇupāliūṇa taṁ puṇa niraīyāraṁ samāhiṇā aṁtē । aṇasaṇavihiṇā mariuṁ pattō sōhamma kappammi ॥ 63 ॥ 6717॥
tattō ya cavittāṇaṁ kulēsu uggēsu hōiuṁ pacchā । sōkkhaparaṁparaēṇaṁ vaccissai mōkkhasōkkhammi” ॥64॥6718॥
ēsō vi tumha kahiō aṇatthadaṁḍavvayassa visayammi । jō pattō dukhāī samiddhadattō tti nāmēṇa ॥ 65 ॥ 6719॥
sikkhāvayāiṁ ēttō bhō bhō ! sāhēmi tumha nisuṇēha । sāmāiyaṁ tu paḍhamaṁ hōi vayaṁ tāṇa majjhammi ||1|| 6720 ||

sāmāiyammi u kaē samaṇasaricchō u sāvaō hōi । tamhā ṇijjaramūlaṁ karēha sāmāiyaṁ bahusō || 3 || 6722॥
kiṁtu iha aiyārā paṁca imē hōṁti vajraṇijā u । maṇa- vai-kāyāṇa ihaṁ duppaṇihāṇaṁ na kāyavvaṁ || 4 || 6723 ॥
sāmaiya saiakaraṇaṁ tahēva aṇavadviyassa karaṇaṁ tu । aiyārarahiyamēyaṁ, annaha sāmāiyaṁ na bhavē || 5 | 6 724 ॥
gihittā sāmaiyaṁ gihavāvārē u ciṁtaē jō u । aṭṭavasaṭṭassa taō niratthayaṁ hōi sāmaiyaṁ || 6 || 6725 ॥
ēyammi u puṇa suddhē kaṁtē nicchiēṇa cittēṇa । hōi suhaṁ jīvāṇaṁ jaha pattaṁ sīhasaḍūḍhēṇa ॥7॥6726 ॥
ābaddha karayalapuḍā parisā vinnavai 'sāmi ! kō ēsō । jō tumhēhiṁ bhaṇiō susāvaō sīhanāmō ?' tti ॥ 8॥6727॥
bhaṇai sirisaṁtināhō "bharahē ramaṇijjapaṭṭaṇē rammē । atthi nivō guṇakaliō sūrō hēmaṁgaō nāma ॥ 1 ॥6728 ॥
hēmasirīnāmēṇa bhajjā tassa'tthi pavarasuhabhāvā । annō vi tattha nivasai saḍūḍhō jiṇadēvanāmō tti || 2 ||6729॥
jiṇadāsīnāmēṇa bhajjā tassa'tthi sayalajiṇabhattā । sā annayā ya pasavai varaputtaṁ sīhayaṁ nāma || 3 ||6730॥
bālayakālē vi imō muṇīṇa pāsammi suṇai varadhammaṁ । bhāvai ya tēṇa cittaṁ, gēṇhai ya vayāī savvāī || 4 ||6731॥
pālai ya niraiyāraṁ bhāvēṇa imō sayā pavaḍūḍhatō । ēvaṁ baccai kālō sāmāiyamāinirayassa || 5 ||6732॥
nāūṇa jōvvaṇatthaṁ pariṇāvai sōhaṇaṁ taō kannaṁ । nāmēṇaṁ paumasiriṁ rūvāisamanniyaṁ jaṇaō || 6 ||6733॥
